 Hindu, Muslim and Christian is for everyone
 Equal law: Women and men get equal property in Goa
 Demand for a uniform civil code has been going on for a long time in India
 desh kii sarvocch adaalat bhi sarkaar se uniform civil code banane ko kah chuki he, lekin abhi tak desh ke nagarikon ko uniform civil code nahin mila he
 At the same time, the Uniform Civil Code is applicable in Goa
 goa hindustan kaa akelaa rajya he, jahaan par uniform civil code lagu he
 Goa has special state status in the Indian Constitution
 saath hi sansad ne kanoon banaakar goa ko portugali civil code lagu karne kaa adhikaar diya tha
 This civil code is still in force in Goa today
 isko goa civil code ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 Let us tell you that Goa joined India in the year 1961
 goa main hindu, muslim or isai samet sabhi dharm or jatiyon ke liye ek family lau he
 This means that the laws of marriage, divorce and succession in Goa are the same for all Hindus, Muslims and Christians
 goa main kisi muslim ko teen baar bolkar apni patni ko talaak dene kaa haq nahin hai
 After registration it is legally valid
 In Goa, people of Muslim, Hindu and Christian communities have the right to marry according to the custom of their religion, but the marriage will be valid only when it is registered
 agar goa main ek baar shaadi kaa registration ho jaataa he, to talaak sirf court se hi miltaa he
 Suppose that if the marriage of a Muslim couple is registered in Goa, they will have to go to court for divorce
 koi bhi muslim apni patni ko bolkar talaak nahin de saktaa he
 This means that Goa does not have a separate personal law for Muslims
 isi tarah hindu or isai samudaay ke log bhi apane reeti-rivaaj ke anusaar shaadi kar sakate hai, lekin registration hone ke baad hi shaadi maanya hoti he
 After this, if there is a reason for divorce for some reason, then one has to go to court
 goa main bina court kii ijaajat ke koi kisi ko talaak nahin de saktaa he
 Women and men get equal rights on property
 Similarly in Goa, spouses of all religions get equal rights on property before marriage and after marriage
 hindu, muslim or isai ke liye alag-alag uttaradhikaar kanoon nahin hai
 The Supreme Court has also praised the Goa Civil Code
 aapako bataa den ki goa ko chhodkar puure desh main hindu, muslim or isai dharm ke logon ke liye alag-alag personal lau hai

 Responding to a question about the surgical strike, Congress leader Milind Deora said that the only bold move (bold step) of the Modi government during the two-and-a-half-year tenure was the targeted strike (surgical strike)
 iskaa bhi kaaphi raajnneetikaran kiya gaya
 He said the attack on terrorist camps in Pakistan-occupied Kashmir across the Line of Control was in fact an attempt to tarnish the image of the central government

 Milind Deora said that in the context of Pakistan, there were many changes in the foreign policy of the Modi government and there were many ups and downs
